Palace – A palace typically refers to the residence and buildings used by a monarch, and can consist of one or more buildings. In Chinese, it was originally a specific term for buildings used by the monarch (emperor, king). Generally, the main building used for ceremonies and official business was called a "dian," while the living quarters were called "gong." In Western countries, "palace" generally refers to the residence of monarchs, nobles, bishops, or important public figures.

*Empresses in the Palace* (also known as *The Legend of Zhen Huan*) is a 2011 Chinese historical drama series set in the Qing Dynasty. Starring Sun Li, Chen Jianbin, Ada Choi, Li Dongxue, Liu Xuehua, Jiang Xin, Li Tianzhu, Tao Xinran, Lan Xi, Zhang Xiaolong, Lan Yingying, Sun Qian, and Zhan Jingyi, the series is adapted from the novel of the same name by Liu Lianzi. Directed by Zheng Xiaolong, with Liu Lianzi and Wang Xiaoping as screenwriters, the series changed the historical setting from the fictional era of the original novel to the reign of Emperor Yongzheng in the Qing Dynasty. The story follows Zhen Huan, who enters the palace through the imperial concubine selection process and experiences the turbulent court life, transforming from naive and innocent to shrewd and cunning, ultimately becoming Empress Dowager, yet still ultimately feeling like a tragic figure in history. Critics praised the series for its complex portrayal of human nature and meticulous historical depiction, but it also faced accusations of plagiarism and controversy regarding its values. *Empresses in the Palace* achieved high viewership ratings and was frequently rebroadcast after its release in mainland China and Taiwan, and is considered one of the most influential Chinese-language drama series in television history.

Chinese Classics---

Dream of the Red Chamber--- Also known as *The Story of the Stone*, *Dream of the Red Chamber* is a classic Chinese novel, considered one of the Four Great Classical Novels. Other names mentioned within the book include *The Record of the Amorous Monk*, *The Golden Jade Bond*, *The Mirror of Love and Lust*, and *The Twelve Beauties of Jinling*. The story begins with a stone left over from Nuwa's mending of the heavens. Unable to mend the heavens, it enters the mortal world with the attendant Shenying, transforming into Jia Baoyu and the jade he was given at birth (Jia Baoyu being the "fake Baoyu"). They travel the world before finally returning to the Great Wilderness, hence the name *The Story of the Stone*. The version with a preface by the Master of Dreams in the 49th year of the Qianlong reign (1784) is titled *Dream of the Red Chamber* (the Jia Chen Dream Preface Manuscript). After the first movable type printing in 1791, *Dream of the Red Chamber* replaced *The Story of the Stone* as the commonly used title.
